2022-12-27T11:37:08.7676460Z   #   setuptools doesn'"'"'t think the script is `-c`. This avoids the following warning:
2022-12-27T11:37:08.7676740Z   #     manifest_maker: standard file '"'"'-c'"'"' not found".
